msg:I visited Wuzhen on the eve of May Day this year and stayed at Yiyuan Boutique. I was generally satisfied and had the following feelings:
Good aspects:
1. The environment is quiet and private. It is located in the core position of the central and southern part of the scenic area. There is a private garden and the rooms on the first floor are facing the water.
2. Western breakfast, three adult packages + one children's package, rich in content, can also be replaced by the morning tea guests in the scenic area from 7:30 to 9:30 (unlimited self-service, ordinary limit is 30/person), or it will be reserved for lunch, until 12:00 on the same day.
3. It is specially pointed out that all service staff are online, with one-to-one butler docking. There are inquiries about room cleaning before each trip (according to personal needs), and they will answer any questions.
Things to note:
If you choose a room on the first floor facing the water, pay attention to choosing a room other than the Pillow Water Inn opposite, so that you will not be easily affected by the working sound in the morning. If you have good sleep quality, you can ignore this point, and the flaws do not outweigh the merits.
